msg:The location is OK, right at the airport, very convenient
The hardware is OK, the overall design is very good
But the details... the thinking of guests is still different from traditional old hotels
For example, the elevator, the floor button will light up after swiping the card, making you think that you don‚Äôt need to press it again to run... But in fact, you have to press it again after swiping the card... Other hotels generally swipe the card and press the button before the button lights up, so there will be no messing around in the elevator
After going up to the floor, the room number indication is not on the wall in front of the elevator, but in the four corners... You have to find the number plate in each of the four corners, and then you know where to turn...
There will be no waiter to guide to the table and pour coffee for breakfast...
It is recommended that the hotel not only do a good job of appearance, but also do a good job of inside... Look at things more from the perspective of guests...

The hotel facilities are basically similar to those of a four-star hotel, with a good swimming pool, fitness center, restaurant, meeting room, bar, etc. The guest rooms of the hotel are relatively small, only more than 30 square meters, which is about the same size as a high-end express hotel, but the interior design is more fashionable, and the electronic equipment is more advanced, and the lights, curtains, TV, etc. can be controlled by voice. Generally speaking, the hotel has an absolute advantage over Atour next door. Hilton has an absolute advantage in terms of location. It also has a swimming pool in the facilities. Although there are some shortcomings in other aspects, the service makes up for it well. It is a good choice.

name:G‚Äçu‚Äçe‚Äçs‚Äçt‚Äç ‚ÄçU‚Äçs‚Äçe‚Äçr
info:Standard Double Room
info:Stayed in July 2023

rating:1
posted:Posted July 20, 2023
msg:This is my first time writing a review on the platform. I hope it will be helpful to people who want to stay here. Because there was a flight to Daxing Airport early the next morning, I checked into the nearest Kapok Hotel with good reviews one day in advance. The two cars arrived in the evening in nearly two hours. The air tickets were also booked on Ctrip, so when I booked the hotel, I found that it was automatically linked to the hotel after the booking was made, thinking that the hotel would arrange a drop-off based on the information. We stayed next to the airport so we wouldn't miss our flight. When we arrived at the hotel, first of all, we had large and small luggage and there were children and the elderly. No one from the hotel came to help. Two well-dressed people came out and stood still and didn't help. I thought they were guests. , seeing us struggling to come over to help, it turned out to be a hotel staff member. Second, go to the front desk to check in. I once again emphasized that the flight information for the next morning required drop-off. The staff told me that it could be done one to one and a half hours in advance. The staff told them that the shuttle bus could only deliver to the middle location, and there was no luggage trolley at the middle delivery location, so you had to carry your luggage and walk more than 200 meters. Our luggage was heavy and heavy, and there were elderly people and children. Finally, after many requests, we agreed to arrange for the staff to help us push our luggage to the entrance of the terminal. Third, because the child cannot sleep well, he will turn over 360 degrees and fall under the bed if not blocked. Their floor is hard. I hope they can provide a mat or two extra quilts on the floor for the child to sleep on. As a result, the lady who answered the phone said that there were no mattresses and we only had one quilt in each room. So I asked if the check-out guest accidentally gets the quilt wet or the child wets the bed due to red wine, how will the next guest stay? Who answered the phone The lady was very sure and said in an argumentative tone that we have the ability to handle it. I suggest you don't rush to argue with the customer seriously. This attitude is not appropriate. So if the quilt suddenly gets wet at night, won't there be a change? No emergency response plan? She would also argue that we can handle it anyway if we have the ability. A girl who talks nonsense. I could only say okay and hang up. In the end, maybe I felt like I had a bad attitude, so I gave her two quilts. The hotel slaps itself in the face. Fourthly, I travel for business and fly all the year round. I usually prepare in advance. My luggage is packed in advance at night. We get up two hours early the next day. Maybe I mentally think that the hotel will arrange a proper drop-off and think that it will remind guests like other hotels. , there is no reality. We called an hour and a half in advance to bring our luggage downstairs, but the front desk who answered the phone said that the car was taking other guests off now and they had to wait. I said, can you just take the luggage off alone? We said just pull our bags downstairs and head to the airport. Then I told them the flight information, brought my luggage downstairs, handed the card to the front desk, and explained the situation again. It turned out that the hotel did not hand over the airport drop-off arrangements promised yesterday to the relevant personnel at all. Two men helped me load my luggage into the trolley at the front desk. I didn‚Äôt want to worry about it anymore. We also had old people and children, so we insisted on letting them go. The two carts were full of luggage, and only one man helped push them. As a result, they walked slower than us old people and children, so he walked slowly behind us. Stop when you reach the middle location, which is where the hotel battery car arrives, not outside the terminal. We saw that he was reluctant to continue, so we pushed it ourselves. We found that there were many trolleys there, but yesterday the hotel said that there were no trolleys where the battery trolleys were parked! ! It is recommended that we push the trolley directly from the hotel front desk. Speechless. Time was already very tight, so we hurriedly pushed in to find the terminal and asked about the check-in location. When we arrived at the check-in location, there was only more than half an hour left, and we still had to queue up. When we found the staff, we were informed that we had priority and had to queue up with those in front. Customers asked one by one if they could move us in advance. At this time, they found another staff member and told them that there was only 25 minutes left and it was too late to take off. You can only cancel the flight, and the ticket cancellation fee for 5 people is high, and there is only one flight per day, and there is no possibility of changing the flight. The elderly and children were very tired, so I could only buy a connecting flight ticket at a high price.
I take countless flights every year, domestic and international flights, and miss a flight for the first time in my life.

Summarize:
The hotel only has some special decorations to attract internet celebrities, such as fully automatic toilets, an unusual lobby design, and there are almost no people in the expensive cultural and creative shops. I have stayed in so many international hotels in various countries. In fact, the details and services of Kapok Hotel are far inferior to that of a three-star hotel. The price is comparable to that of a five-star hotel in this remote location.
It is recommended not to rely on the hotel drop-off service. These staff have not received professional training. Compared with the Guoerzhao Hotel where we just stayed, the service level is that of a B&B (some B&Bs may do better). Like temporary staff cobbled together here and there, listless.
The above is our actual accommodation experience, I hope it can help others who will stay later.
